TRIAL WINNING DECKLISTS
=======================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on March 14, 2015 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/hero/news_default_wizards_logo_0.jpg)
By Jacob Van Lunen and Adam Styborski 










Hundreds of players attempted to earn themselves a few byes by entering Grand Prix trials yesterday. It's no surprise to see strategies like Mardu and Abzan winning these events, but it's quite extraordinary to see strategies like Naya performing well in this Sealed Deck environment. It seems that mana fixing has a major influence on deck construction for the players with the most success. Let's check out the undefeated Grand Prix Trial decklists from Cleveland.







#### Thomas Foley â€“ Mardu


##### 




[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)](/en/decklist/deck-list-e9243eff864a2e2d013791edbed27be5?n=Thomas%20Foley%20%E2%80%93%20Mardu)

#### Ronnie Ritter â€“ Five-Color
